;;; Truth functions
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_c2w',C],[/,C,[-,1,C]]])
(= 
  (Truth_c2w $C) 
  (/ $C 
    (- 1 $C)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_w2c',W],[/,W,[+,W,1]]])
(= 
  (Truth_w2c $W) 
  (/ $W 
    (+ $W 1)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Deduction',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,F2],[*,[*,F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]]])
(= 
  (Truth_Deduction 
    ($F1 $C1) 
    ($F2 $C2)) 
  ( (* $F1 $F2) 
    (* 
      (* $F1 $F2) 
      (* $C1 $C2))))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Abduction',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[F2,['Truth_w2c',[*,[*,F1,C1],C2]]]])
(= 
  (Truth_Abduction 
    ($F1 $C1) 
    ($F2 $C2)) 
  ($F2 
    (Truth_w2c 
      (* 
        (* $F1 $C1) $C2))))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Induction',T1,T2],['Truth_Abduction',T2,T1]])
(= 
  (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2) 
  (Truth_Abduction $T2 $T1))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Exemplification',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[1.0,['Truth_w2c',[*,[*,F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]]]])
(= 
  (Truth_Exemplification 
    ($F1 $C1) 
    ($F2 $C2)) 
  (1.0 
    (Truth_w2c 
      (* 
        (* $F1 $F2) 
        (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T],['Truth_Deduction',T,[1.0,0.9]]])
(= 
  (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T) 
  (Truth_Deduction $T 
    (1.0 0.9)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Negation',[F,C]],[[-,1,F],C]])
(= 
  (Truth_Negation 
    ($F $C)) 
  ( (- 1 $F) $C))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth','StructuralDeductionNegated',T],['Truth_Negation',['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_or',A,B],[-,1,[*,[-,1,A],[-,1,B]]]])
(=

  (- 1 
    (* 
      (- 1 $A) 
      (- 1 $B))))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Comparison',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,F0,['Truth_or',F1,F2],[['If',[==,F0,0.0],0.0,[/,[*,F1,F2],F0]],['Truth_w2c',[*,F0,[*,C1,C2]]]]]])
(= 
  (Truth_Comparison 
    ($F1 $C1) 
    ($F2 $C2))

          (* $F1 $F2) $F0)) 
      (Truth_w2c 
        (* $F0 
          (* $C1 $C2))))))

;;;NAL-1
;;;!Syllogistic rules for Inheritance:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,B],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[A,-->,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A --> $B) $T1) 
    ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($A --> $C) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,B],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[C,-->,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A --> $B) $T1) 
    ( ($A --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($C --> $B) 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,C],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[B,-->,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A --> $C) $T1) 
    ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($B --> $A) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,B],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Exemplification',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A --> $B) $T1) 
    ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($C --> $A) 
    (Truth_Exemplification $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL-2

(=

  ( ($P <-> $S) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,<->,P],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[S,<->,P],['Truth_Resemblance',T1,T2]]])

    ( ($S <-> $M) $T2))

    (Truth_Resemblance $T1 $T2)))



  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,-->,M],T2]],[[S,<->,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S --> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <-> $P) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,S],T2]],[[S,<->,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M --> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <-> $P) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[S,-->,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S --> $P) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,S],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($P --> $S) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Dealing with properties and instances:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,['{...}',['$P']]],T]],[[S,<->,['{...}',['$P']]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($S --> 
        { $P }) $T)) 
          ( ($S <-> 
              { $P }) 
                (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[['[...]',['$S']]],-->,P],T]],[[[['[...]',['$S']]],<->,P],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ( [ $S ]) --> $P) $T)) 
            ( ( ( [ $S ]) <-> $P) 
                    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$M']],-->,P],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[['{...}',['$S']],-->,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( { $M } --> $P) $T1) 
          ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
          ( ( { $S } --> $P) 
                (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,[['[...]',['$M']]]],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,[['[...]',['$S']]]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> 
        ( [ $M ])) $T1) 
            ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
            ( ($P --> 
                ( [ $S ])) 
                    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A']],<->,['{...}',['$B']]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( { $A } <-> 
          { $B })) 
            ($A <-> $B) 
            (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[['[...]',['$A']]],<->,[['[...]',['$B']]]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ( [ $A ]) <-> 
            ( [ $B ]))) 
                ($A <-> $B) 
                (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])

    ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
  ($B 
    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[[B,&&,A],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
  ( ($B && $A) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[S,&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($S $T1) 
    ( ($S && $A) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[S,'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($S $T1) 
    ( ($S || $A) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNNN',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($S $T1) 
    ( ( (! $S) && $A) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_DecomposeNNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePPP',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($S $T1) 
    ( ( (! $S) || $A) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_DecomposePPP $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Syllogistic rules for Implication:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[A,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($A ==> $C) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[A,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
    ( ($A ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> $B) 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($B ==> $A) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,A],['Truth_Exemplification',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> $A) 
    (Truth_Exemplification $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Conditional composition for conjunction and disjunction:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) 
    (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,'||',B],==>,C],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($A || $B) ==> $C) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,&&,B]],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
    ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> 
      ($A && $B)) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,'||',B]],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
    ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> 
      ($A || $B)) 
    (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Multi-conditional inference:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[S,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[P,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($S && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
  ($P 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[[C,&&,S],==>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($C && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
    ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S ==> $P) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Rules for equivalence:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,<=>,P],T]],[[P,<=>,S],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($S <=> $P) $T)) 
  ( ($P <=> $S) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,==>,P],T1],[[P,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($S ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($P ==> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <=> $P) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <=> $P) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <=> $P) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S ==> $P) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[P,==>,S],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($P ==> $S) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,<=>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Resemblance',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M <=> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ($S <=> $P) 
    (Truth_Resemblance $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Higher-order decomposition
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($A $T1) 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ($B 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($A $T1) 
    ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($B ==> $C) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[B,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[A,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($B $T1) 
    ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[A,<=>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ($A $T1) 
    ( ($A <=> $B) $T2)) 
  ($B 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL term reductions
;;;!Extensional intersection, union, conjunction reductions:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,&,A],A])
(= 
  ($A & $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,'|',A],A])
(= 
  ($A | $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,&&,A],A])
(= 
  ($A && $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,'||',A],A])
(= 
  ($A || $A) $A)


;;;!Extensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[A]],'|',['{...}',[B]]],['{...}',[A,B]]])
(= 
  ( { $A } | 
      { $B }) 
        { $A $B })


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[A,B]],'|',['{...}',[C]]],['{...}',[[A|B],C]]])
(= 
  ( { $A $B } | 
      { $C }) 
        { (Cons  $A $B) $C })


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[C]],'|',['{...}',[A,B]]],['{...}',[C,[A|B]]]])
(= 
  ( { $C } | 
      { $A $B }) 
        { $C 
          (Cons  $A $B) })


;;;!Intensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A]]],&,[['[...]',[B]]]],[['[...]',[A,B]]]])
(= 
  ( ( [ $A ]) & 
        ( [ $B ])) 
            ( [ $A $B ]))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A,B]]],&,[['[...]',[C]]]],[['[...]',[[A|B],C]]]])
(= 
  ( ( [ $A $B ]) & 
        ( [ $C ])) 
            ( [ (Cons  $A $B) $C ]))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A]]],&,[['[...]',[B,C]]]],[['[...]',[A,[B|C]]]]])
(= 
  ( ( [ $A ]) & 
        ( [ $B $C ])) 
            ( [ $A 
                (Cons  $B $C) ]))


;;;!Reduction for set element copula:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['{...}',[[A|B]]],['{...}',[A,B]]])
(= 
  { (Cons  $A $B) } 
    { $A $B })


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[['[...]',[[A|B]]]],[['[...]',[A,B]]]])
(= 
  ( [ (Cons  $A $B) ]) 
      ( [ $A $B ]))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BestCandidate',Tuple,EvaluateCandidateFunction,T],[sequential,[[do,['change-state!','&tempbestscore',0]],[do,['change-state!','&tempbest','Nil']],[do,['let*',[[X,[superpose,Tuple]],[Fx,[EvaluateCandidateFunction,X,T]]],[superpose,[['If',[>,Fx,['get-state','&tempbestscore']],[sequential,[['change-state!','&tempbest',X],['change-state!','&tempbestscore',Fx]]]]]]]],['get-state','&tempbest']]]])

        (change-state! &tempbestscore 0))

                (> $Fx 
                  (get-state &tempbestscore)) 
                (sequential 
                  ( (change-state! &tempbest $X) 
                    (change-state! &tempbestscore $Fx)))))))) 
      (get-state &tempbest))))

;;bound the size of the attentional focus for tasks / events
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BoundEvents',Collection,Threshold,Increment,TargetAmount,T],[sequential,[[do,['let*',[[Ev,['get-atoms',Collection]],[['Event',Sentence,[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],Ev]],['If',[<,['EventPriorityNow',EPrio,T],Threshold],['remove-atom',Collection,Ev]]]],[let,CurrentAmount,['CollapseCardinality',['get-atoms',Collection]],['If',[>,CurrentAmount,TargetAmount],['BoundEvents',Collection,[+,Threshold,Increment],Increment,TargetAmount,T]]]]]])
(= 
  (BoundEvents $Collection $Threshold $Increment $TargetAmount $T) 
  (sequential 
    ( (do 
        (let* 
          ( ($Ev 
              (get-atoms $Collection)) 
            ( (Event $Sentence 
                ($Time $Evidence $EPrio)) $Ev)) 
          (If 
            (< 
              (EventPriorityNow $EPrio $T) $Threshold) 
            (remove-atom $Collection $Ev)))) 
      (let $CurrentAmount 
        (CollapseCardinality 
          (get-atoms $Collection)) 
        (If 
          (> $CurrentAmount $TargetAmount) 
          (BoundEvents $Collection 
            (+ $Threshold $Increment) $Increment $TargetAmount $T))))))

        (get-state &tempstate)))))


;;revise if there is no evidential overlap, else use higher-confident candidate
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['RevisionAndChoice',['Event',[Term1,[F1,C1]],[eternal,Ev1,EPrio1]],['Event',[Term2,[F2,C2]],[eternal,Ev2,EPrio2]]],[let,ConclusionStamp,['TupleConcat',Ev1,Ev2],['If',['StampDisjoint',ConclusionStamp],['Event',[Term1,['Truth_Revision',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]]],[eternal,ConclusionStamp,[0,0.0]]],['If',[>,C1,C2],['Event',[Term1,[F1,C1]],[eternal,Ev1,[0,0.0]]],['Event',[Term2,[F2,C2]],[eternal,Ev2,[0,0.0]]]]]]])
(= 
  (RevisionAndChoice 
    (Event 
      ($Term1 
        ($F1 $C1)) 
      (eternal $Ev1 $EPrio1)) 
    (Event 
      ($Term2 
        ($F2 $C2)) 
      (eternal $Ev2 $EPrio2))) 
  (let $ConclusionStamp 
    (TupleConcat $Ev1 $Ev2) 
    (If 
      (StampDisjoint $ConclusionStamp) 
      (Event 
        ($Term1 
          (Truth_Revision 
            ($F1 $C1) 
            ($F2 $C2))) 
        (eternal $ConclusionStamp 
          (0 0.0))) 
      (If 
        (> $C1 $C2) 
        (Event 
          ($Term1 
            ($F1 $C1)) 
          (eternal $Ev1 
            (0 0.0))) 
        (Event 
          ($Term2 
            ($F2 $C2)) 
          (eternal $Ev2 
            (0 0.0)))))))


;;update beliefs in existing concept with the new event or create new concept to enter the new evidence
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['UpdateConcept',NewEvent,T],['let*',[[['Event',[Term,TV],[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],NewEvent],[NewEventEternalized,['Eternalize',NewEvent]],[MatchConcept,['Concept',Term,Belief,BeliefEvent,CPrio]]],[sequential,[[case,[match,'&attentional_focus',MatchConcept,MatchConcept],[[MatchConcept,[sequential,[['remove-atom','&attentional_focus',MatchConcept],['let*',[[['Event',RevSentence,Metadata],['RevisionAndChoice',Belief,NewEventEternalized]],[RevisedBelief,['Event',['trace!',[@,RevSentence],RevSentence],Metadata]],[MaxPrio,['If',[>,['EventPriorityNow',EPrio,T],['ConceptPriorityNow',CPrio,T]],EPrio,CPrio]]],['add-atom','&attentional_focus',['Concept',Term,RevisedBelief,NewEvent,MaxPrio]]]]]],['%void%',[case,[match,'&concepts',MatchConcept,MatchConcept],[[MatchConcept,[sequential,[['remove-atom','&concepts',MatchConcept],['add-atom','&attentional_focus',MatchConcept],['UpdateConcept',NewEvent,T]]]],['%void%',['add-atom','&attentional_focus',['Concept',Term,NewEventEternalized,NewEvent,EPrio]]]]]]]]]]]])
(= 
  (UpdateConcept $NewEvent $T) 
  (let* 
    ( ( (Event 
          ($Term $TV) 
          ($Time $Evidence $EPrio)) $NewEvent) 
      ($NewEventEternalized 
        (Eternalize $NewEvent)) 
      ($MatchConcept 
        (Concept $Term $Belief $BeliefEvent $CPrio))) 
    (sequential 
      ( (case 
          (match &attentional_focus $MatchConcept $MatchConcept) 
          ( ($MatchConcept 
              (sequential 
                ( (remove-atom &attentional_focus $MatchConcept) 
                  (let* 
                    ( ( (Event $RevSentence $Metadata) 
                        (RevisionAndChoice $Belief $NewEventEternalized)) 
                      ($RevisedBelief 
                        (Event 
                          (trace! 
                            (@ $RevSentence) $RevSentence) $Metadata)) 
                      ($MaxPrio 
                        (If 
                          (> 
                            (EventPriorityNow $EPrio $T) 
                            (ConceptPriorityNow $CPrio $T)) $EPrio $CPrio))) 
                    (add-atom &attentional_focus 
                      (Concept $Term $RevisedBelief $NewEvent $MaxPrio)))))) 
            (%void% 
              (case 
                (match &concepts $MatchConcept $MatchConcept) 
                ( ($MatchConcept 
                    (sequential 
                      ( (remove-atom &concepts $MatchConcept) 
                        (add-atom &attentional_focus $MatchConcept) 
                        (UpdateConcept $NewEvent $T)))) 
                  (%void% 
                    (add-atom &attentional_focus 
                      (Concept $Term $NewEventEternalized $NewEvent $EPrio))))))))))))


;;bound the size of attentional focus of concepts
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BoundAttention',Threshold,Increment,TargetAmount,T],[sequential,[[do,['let*',[[C,['get-atoms','&attentional_focus']],[['Concept',Term,['Event',Sentence,Metadata],BeliefEvent,CPrio],C]],['If',[<,['ConceptPriorityNow',CPrio,T],Threshold],[sequential,[['remove-atom','&attentional_focus',C],['add-atom','&concepts',C]]]]]],[let,CurrentAmount,['CollapseCardinality',['get-atoms','&attentional_focus']],['If',[>,CurrentAmount,TargetAmount],['BoundAttention',[+,Threshold,Increment],Increment,TargetAmount,T]]]]]])
(= 
  (BoundAttention $Threshold $Increment $TargetAmount $T) 
  (sequential 
    ( (do 
        (let* 
          ( ($C 
              (get-atoms &attentional_focus)) 
            ( (Concept $Term 
                (Event $Sentence $Metadata) $BeliefEvent $CPrio) $C)) 
          (If 
            (< 
              (ConceptPriorityNow $CPrio $T) $Threshold) 
            (sequential 
              ( (remove-atom &attentional_focus $C) 
                (add-atom &concepts $C)))))) 
      (let $CurrentAmount 
        (CollapseCardinality 
          (get-atoms &attentional_focus)) 
        (If 
          (> $CurrentAmount $TargetAmount) 
          (BoundAttention 
            (+ $Threshold $Increment) $Increment $TargetAmount $T))))))

;;making declarative inferences on two events (task from PQ and belief from concept)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Conclude',['Event',S1,[Time1,Ev1,Prio1]],['Event',S2,[Time2,Ev2,Prio2]],CPrio,T],[let,ConclusionStamp,['TupleConcat',Ev1,Ev2],['If',['StampDisjoint',ConclusionStamp],[let,[ConcTerm,ConcTV],[superpose,[['|-',S1,S2],['|-',S2,S1]]],['Event',[ConcTerm,ConcTV],[Time1,ConclusionStamp,[T,['ConclusionPriority',['EventPriorityNow',Prio1,T],['ConceptPriorityNow',CPrio,T],ConcTV]]]]]]]])
(= 
  (Conclude 
    (Event $S1 
      ($Time1 $Ev1 $Prio1)) 
    (Event $S2 
      ($Time2 $Ev2 $Prio2)) $CPrio $T) 
  (let $ConclusionStamp 
    (TupleConcat $Ev1 $Ev2) 
    (If 
      (StampDisjoint $ConclusionStamp) 
      (let 
        ($ConcTerm $ConcTV) 
        (superpose 
          ( (|- $S1 $S2) 
            (|- $S2 $S1))) 
        (Event 
          ($ConcTerm $ConcTV) 
          ($Time1 $ConclusionStamp 
            ($T 
              (ConclusionPriority 
                (EventPriorityNow $Prio1 $T) 
                (ConceptPriorityNow $CPrio $T) $ConcTV))))))))


;;find a belief for the task to generate conclusions with
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['ReasonWithTask',['Event',S1,[Time1,Ev1,Prio1]],T],[let,[Belief,CPrio],[case,['get-atoms','&attentional_focus'],[[['Concept',Term,['Event',SE2,[TimeE2,EvE2,PrioE2]],['Event',S2,[Time2,Ev2,Prio2]],CPrio],['If',[and,[not,[==,Time1,eternal]],[>,[abs,[-,Time1,Time2]],20]],[['Event',SE2,[TimeE2,EvE2,PrioE2]],Cprio],[['Event',S2,[Time2,Ev2,Prio2]],CPrio]]]]],[case,['Conclude',['Event',S1,[Time1,Ev1,Prio1]],['TemporallyAlignedBelief',Time1,Belief],CPrio,T],[[['Event',Num1,Num2],['ProcessBeliefEvent',['Event',['trace!',['.',Num1],Num1],Num2],T]]]]]])
(= 
  (ReasonWithTask 
    (Event $S1 
      ($Time1 $Ev1 $Prio1)) $T)

              ($TimeE2 $EvE2 $PrioE2))

              ($Time2 $Ev2 $Prio2)) $CPrio)

            (and 
              (not 
                (== $Time1 eternal)) 
              (> 
                (abs 
                  (- $Time1 $Time2)) 20))

                ($TimeE2 $EvE2 $PrioE2)) $Cprio) 
            ( (Event $S2 
                ($Time2 $Ev2 $Prio2)) $CPrio))))) 
    (case 
      (Conclude 
        (Event $S1 
          ($Time1 $Ev1 $Prio1)) 
        (TemporallyAlignedBelief $Time1 $Belief) $CPrio $T) 
      ( ( (Event $Num1 $Num2) 
          (ProcessBeliefEvent 
            (Event 
              (trace! 
                (. $Num1) $Num1) $Num2) $T))))))


;;select the highest priority belief event from the PQ and use it for reasoning
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BeliefCycle',T],[do,[sequential,[[let,Ev,['SelectHighestPriorityEvent','&belief_events',T],[sequential,[['remove-atom','&belief_events',Ev],['ReasonWithTask',Ev,T]]]],['UpdateReasonerState'],['BoundEvents','&belief_events',0.0,0.1,['BeliefEventsMax'],T],['BoundAttention',0.0,0.1,['AttentionalFocusConceptsMax'],T]]]]])

        (BoundEvents &belief_events 0.0 0.1 
          (BeliefEventsMax) $T) 
        (BoundAttention 0.0 0.1 
          (AttentionalFocusConceptsMax) $T)))))


;;;Temporal inference (sequence and implication formation based on FIFO)
;;use the event's evidence to induce a time-independent belief which can be used in the future
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Eternalize',Ev],[let,['Event',[Term,TV],[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],Ev,['If',[==,Time,eternal],Ev,['Event',[Term,['Truth_Eternalize',TV]],[eternal,Evidence,[0,0.0]]]]]])

          (Truth_Eternalize $TV)) 
        (eternal $Evidence 
          (0 0.0))))))

;;Find implications in the event FIFO:
;;procedural implications
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['TemporalImplicationInduction',[Cons,Op,Prec]],['If',[and,['IsOp',Op],[and,[not,['IsOp',Cons]],[not,['IsOp',Prec]]]],[let,PrecOp,['TemporalSequence',Prec,Op],['TemporalImplication',PrecOp,Cons]]]])

;;Input procedure
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['AddBeliefEvent',Sentence],['let*',[[[T,EvidentialBase],['GetReasonerState']],[InputEvent,['Event',['trace!',['.',Sentence],Sentence],[T,EvidentialBase,[T,1.0]]]],[NotAnOperation,[not,['IsOp',InputEvent]]]],[do,[sequential,[['EventToFIFO',InputEvent],['Anticipate',['get-state','&FIFO'],T],['If',NotAnOperation,[sequential,[[let,InducedHypothesis,['TemporalImplicationInduction',['get-state','&FIFO']],['UpdateConcept',InducedHypothesis,T]],['ProcessBeliefEvent',InputEvent,T],['BeliefCycle',T]]],['UpdateReasonerState']]]]]]])

                    (get-state &FIFO))

            (UpdateReasonerState)))))))

;;Add subgoals to the PQ

;;execute the operation which most likely gets the goal achieved in current contexts, and if contexts are not yet fulfilled, derive them as subgoals
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BestDecision',T,['Event',[Term,DV],[GoalTime,GoalEvBase,GoalPrio]],FIFO],[let,Options,[collapse,['let*',[[['Event',[[[Prec,&/,[^,Op]],=/>,Term],ImpTV],[ImpTime,ImpEvBase,ImpPrio]],['EternalQuestion',[[Prec,&/,[^,Op]],=/>,Term]]],[DVPrecOp,['Truth_Deduction',DV,ImpTV]],[['Event',[PrecTerm,PrecTV],PrecMetadata],['Projection',['EventQuestion',Prec],T]],[DVOp,['Truth_Deduction',PrecTV,DVPrecOp]],[DVPrec,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',DVPrecOp]],[SubgoalStamp,['TupleConcat',GoalEvBase,ImpEvBase]]],['If',['StampDisjoint',SubgoalStamp],['Decision',[[^,Op],DVOp],['Event',[Prec,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',DVPrecOp]],[T,SubgoalStamp,[T,['SubgoalPriority',['EventPriorityNow',GoalPrio,T],DVPrec]]]]]]]],[let,['Decision',[Opname,DVOp],Subgoal],['BestCandidate',Options,'OpExpectation',T],['If',[>,['Truth_Expectation',DVOp],0.5],['Execute',Opname],['DeriveSubgoals',Options]]]]])
(= 
  (BestDecision $T 
    (Event 
      ($Term $DV) 
      ($GoalTime $GoalEvBase $GoalPrio)) $FIFO) 
  (let $Options 
    (collapse 
      (let* 
        ( ( (Event 
              ( ( ($Prec &/ 
                    (^ $Op)) =/> $Term) $ImpTV) 
              ($ImpTime $ImpEvBase $ImpPrio)) 
            (EternalQuestion 
              ( ($Prec &/ 
                  (^ $Op)) =/> $Term))) 
          ($DVPrecOp 
            (Truth_Deduction $DV $ImpTV)) 
          ( (Event 
              ($PrecTerm $PrecTV) $PrecMetadata) 
            (Projection 
              (EventQuestion $Prec) $T)) 
          ($DVOp 
            (Truth_Deduction $PrecTV $DVPrecOp)) 
          ($DVPrec 
            (Truth_StructuralDeduction $DVPrecOp)) 
          ($SubgoalStamp 
            (TupleConcat $GoalEvBase $ImpEvBase))) 
        (If 
          (StampDisjoint $SubgoalStamp) 
          (Decision 
            ( (^ $Op) $DVOp) 
            (Event 
              ($Prec 
                (Truth_StructuralDeduction $DVPrecOp)) 
              ($T $SubgoalStamp 
                ($T 
                  (SubgoalPriority 
                    (EventPriorityNow $GoalPrio $T) $DVPrec)))))))) 
    (let 
      (Decision 
        ($Opname $DVOp) $Subgoal) 
      (BestCandidate $Options OpExpectation $T) 
      (If 
        (> 
          (Truth_Expectation $DVOp) 0.5) 
        (Execute $Opname) 
        (DeriveSubgoals $Options)))))


;;select the highest priority goal event from the PQ and use it for decision making
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['GoalCycle',T],[sequential,[[let,Ev,['SelectHighestPriorityEvent','&goal_events',T],[sequential,[[do,['remove-atom','&goal_events',Ev]],['BestDecision',T,Ev,['get-state','&FIFO']]]]],[do,['UpdateReasonerState']],[do,['BoundEvents','&goal_events',0.0,0.1,['GoalEventsMax'],T]]]]])
(= 
  (GoalCycle $T) 
  (sequential 
    ( (let $Ev 
        (SelectHighestPriorityEvent &goal_events $T) 
        (sequential 
          ( (do 
              (remove-atom &goal_events $Ev)) 
            (BestDecision $T $Ev 
              (get-state &FIFO))))) 
      (do 
        (UpdateReasonerState)) 
      (do 
        (BoundEvents &goal_events 0.0 0.1 
          (GoalEventsMax) $T)))))

    (sequential 
      ( (do 
          (add-atom &goal_events $InputEvent)) 
        (GoalCycle $T)))))
